 ;CODE MEMORY: (0x00000000-0x0000FFFF) 
 ;DATA MEMORY: (0x00010000-0x0001FFFF) 

 org 0000 

 mfc0 $16, $13
 beq $16, $0, _reset

 exception_handler: 
	mfc0 $16, $12
	mfc0 $17, $13
	mfc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $20, $15
	sw $16, 0($29)
	sw $17, 4($29)
	sw $19, 8($29)
	sw $20, 12($29)
	addi $19, $19, 4
	mtc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $21, $12
	addi $21, $21, 65533
	ori $21, $21, 1
	mtc0 $21, $12
	cop0 4
	jr $19

 _reset: 
	xor $0, $0, $0
	xor $1, $1, $1

;..........hilo test..........;
jal reset_offsets
jal reset_hi_lo
hilo_register_operation:
	jal init_upward_1
	jal hi_upward_0
	jal hi_downward_1
	jal lo_upward_0
	jal lo_downward_1
	jal init_upward_0
	jal hi_upward_1
	jal hi_downward_0
	jal lo_upward_1
	jal lo_downward_0

 j end

load_patterns:
	lw $15, 0($30)
	lw $16, 4($30)
	jr $31

reset_offsets:
	lui $30, 1
	ori $30, $30, 8
	xor $27, $27, $27
	xor $18, $18, $18
	jr $31

reset_hi_lo:
	mthi $0
	mtlo $0
	jr $31

increment_offset:
	addi $30, $30, 8
	addi $27, $27, 2
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

increment_immediate:
	addi $30, $30, 8
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

increment:
	addi $29, $29, 4
	jr $31

store_branch:
	sw $15, 0($29)
	jr $31

store:
	sw $18, 0($29)
	sw $19, 4($29)
	jr $31

	mtc0 $0, $12
	mtc0 $0, $13
	mtc0 $0, $14
	mtc0 $0, $15
	jr $31
